# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:08:57.847199

### Base Program

```py
def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 1

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def busy_student(start_time, end_time, query_time):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(start_time)):
        if start_time[i] <= query_time <= end_time[i]:
            count += 1
    return count


```
